============================================================================\n-- FUNCTIONS & TRIGGERS\n-- ============================================================================\n\n-- Function to update updated_at timestamp\nCREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()\nRETURNS TRIGGER AS $$\nBEGIN\n    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;\n    RETURN NEW;\nEND;\n$$ language \'plpgsql\';\n\n-- Apply updated_at trigger to all relevant tables\nCREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON users FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\nCREATE TRIGGER update_data_sources_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON data_sources FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\nCREATE TRIGGER update_datasets_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON datasets FOR EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\n-- ============================================================================\n-- VIEWS\n-- ============================================================================\n\n-- View for dashboard statistics\nCREATE OR REPLACE VIEW dashboard_stats AS\nSELECT \n    d.id,\n    d.name,\n    d.created_by,\n    u.full_name as creator_name,\n    COUNT(DISTINCT v.id) as visualization_count,\n    d.created_at,\n    d.updated_at\nFROM dashboards d\nLEFT JOIN visualizations v ON v.dashboard_id = d.id\nLEFT JOIN users u ON u.id = d.created_by\nGROUP BY d.id, d.name, d.created_by, u.full_name, d.created_at, d.updated_at;\n\n-- View for query performance\nCREATE OR REPLACE VIEW query_performance AS\nSELECT \n    q.id,\n    q.name,\n    q.execution_count,\n    q.avg_execution_time,\n    COUNT(qh.id) as history_count,\n    MAX(qh.executed_at) as last_executed,\n    AVG(qh.execution_time) as actual_avg_time\nFROM queries q\nLEFT JOIN query_history qh ON qh.query_id = q.id\nGROUP BY q.id, q.name, q.execution_count, q.avg_execution_time;\n\n-- View for user activity\nCREATE OR REPLACE VIEW user_activity AS\nSELECT \n    u.id,\n    u.username,\n    u.full_name,\n    COUNT(DISTINCT al.id) as action_count,\n    MAX(al.created_at) as last_activity,\n    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN al.action = \'login\' THEN al.id END) as login_count\nFROM users u\nLEFT JOIN audit_logs al ON al.user_id = u.id\nGROUP BY u.id, u.username, u.full_name;\n\n-- **SSL/TLS**: Enable HTTPS\n5. **Firewall**: Configure appropriate rules\n\n---\n\n## Database Setup\n\n### Automatic Initialization\n\nThe PostgreSQL database is automatically initialized with:\n- 15 tables with proper indexes\n- Sample data (3 users, 5 data sources, etc.)\n- Triggers for timestamp updates\n- Views for analytics\n\n### Manual Database Operations\n\n#### Connect to PostgreSQL\n```bash\ndocker-compose exec postgres psql -U pulse_user -d pulse\n```\n\n#### Backup Database\n```bash\ndocker-compose exec postgres pg_dump -U pulse_user pulse > backup.sql\n```\n\n#### Restore Database\n```bash\ndocker-compose exec -T postgres psql -U pulse_user pulse < backup.sql\n```\n\n#### Reset Database\n```bash\ndocker-compose down -v\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n### ClickHouse Setup\n\nClickHouse is automatically initialized with:\n- 8 analytics tables\n- 3 materialized views for aggregations\n- Sample event data\n\n#### Connect to Stop and Remove Volumes\n```bash\ndocker-compose down -v\n```\n\n### Backend Development\n\n#### Run Backend Locally (without Docker)\n```bash\ncd backend\n\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m 8000\n```\n\n#### Run Tests\n```bash\ncd backend\npytest\npytest --cov=. --cov-report=html\n```\n\n### Frontend Development\n\n#### Run Frontend Locally (without Docker)\n```bash\ncd frontend\n\n# Install dependencies\nnpm install\n\n# Run development server\nnpm run dev\n\n# Build for production\nnpm run build\n\n# Preview production build\nnpm run preview\n```\n\n#### Run Tests\n```bash\ncd frontend\nnpm test\nnpm run test:coverage\n```\n\n---\n\n## Production Deployment\n\n### Docker Compose Production\n\n1. **Update docker-compose.prod.yml**:\n```yaml\nversion: \'3.8\'\n\nservices:\n  backend:\n    build:\n      context: ./backend\n      dockerfile: Dockerfile.prod\n    environment:\n      ENVIRONMENT: production\n      DEBUG: "false"\n    restart: always\n    \n  frontend:\n    build:\n      context: ./frontend\n      dockerfile: Dockerfile.prod\n    restart: always\n```\n\n2. **Deploy**:\n```bash\ndocker-compose -f docker-compose.prod.yml up -d\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Deployment\n\n1. **Create Kubernetes manifests** (see `k8s/` directory)\n2. **Deploy**:\n```bash\nkubectl apply -f k8s/namespace.yaml\nkubectl apply -f k8s/configmap.yaml\nkubectl apply -f return 301 https://$server_name$request_uri;\n}\n\nserver {\n    listen 443 ssl http2;\n    server_name pulse.yourdomain.com;\n    \n    ssl_certificate /etc/ssl/certs/pulse.crt;\n --query "SELECT 1"\n```\n\n### Monitoring Tools\n\n#### Prometheus Metrics\n```bash\n# Backend exposes metrics at /metrics\ncurl http://localhost:8000/metrics\n```\n\n#### Log Aggregation\n```bash\n# View aggregated logs\ndocker-compose logs -f --tail=100\n\n# Export logs\ndocker-compose logs > logs.txt\n```\n\n### Backup Strategy\n\n#### Automated Backups\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# backup.sh\n\nDATE=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)\nBACKUP_DIR="/backups"\n\n# PostgreSQL backup\ndocker-compose exec -T postgres pg_dump -U pulse_user pulse > "$BACKUP_DIR/postgres_$DATE.sql"\n\n# ClickHouse backup\ndocker-compose exec -T clickhouse clickhouse-client --query "BACKUP DATABASE analytics TO Disk(\'backups\', \'$DATE\')"\n\n# Compress backups\ntar -czf "$BACKUP_DIR/pulse_backup_$DATE.tar.gz" "$BACKUP_DIR"/*_$DATE.*\n\n# Remove old backups (keep last 30 days)\nfind "$BACKUP_DIR" -name "*.tar.gz" -mtime +30 -delete\n```\n\n#### Restore from Backup\n```bash\n# PostgreSQL restore\ndocker-compose exec -T postgres psql -U pulse_user pulse < backup.sql\n\n# ClickHouse restore\ndocker-compose exec clickhouse clickhouse-client --query "RESTORE DATABASE analytics FROM Disk(\'backups\', \'backup_name\')"\n```\n\n### Performance Tuning\n\n#### PostgreSQL\n```sql\n-- Analyze tables\nANALYZE;\n\n-- Vacuum tables\nVACUUM ANALYZE;\n\n-- Check slow queries\nSELECT * FROM pg_stat_statements ORDER BY mean_exec_time DESC LIMIT 10;\n```\n\n#### ClickHouse\n```sql\n-- Optimize tables\nOPTIMIZE TABLE analytics.events;\n\n-- Check query performance\nSELECT * FROM system.query_log ORDER BY query_duration_ms DESC LIMIT 10;\n```\n\n#### Redis\n```bash\n# Check memory usage\ndocker-compose exec redis redis-cli INFO memory\n\n# Clear cache\ndocker-compose exec redis redis-cli FLUSHALL\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### Port Already in Use\n```bash\n# Find process using port\nlsof -i :8000\nsudo netstat -tulpn | grep :8000\n\n# Kill process\nkill -9 <PID>\n```\n\n#### Container Won\'t Start\n```bash\n# Check logs\ndocker-compose logs <service-name>\n\n# Rebuild container\ndocker-compose build --no-cache <service-name>\ndocker-compose up -d <service-name>\n```\n\n#### Database Connection Failed\n```bash\n# Check if PostgreSQL is running\ndocker-compose ps postgres\n\n# Check connection\ndocker-compose exec postgres psql -U pulse_user -d pulse -c "SELECT 1"\n\n# Reset database\ndocker-compose down -v\ndocker-compose up -d postgres\n```\n\n#### Out of Memory\n```bash\n# Check Docker memory\ndocker stats\n\n# Increase Docker memory limit (Docker Desktop)\n# Settings > Resources > Memory > Increase limit\n\n# Clear unused resources\ndocker system prune -a\n```\n\n#### Frontend Build Fails\n```bash\n# Clear node_modules and reinstall\ncd frontend\nrm -rf node_modules package-lock.json\nnpm install\n\n# Clear cache\nnpm cache clean --force\n```\n\n### Debug Mode\n\n#### Enable Debug Logging\n```bash\n# Backend\nexport DEBUG=true\nexport LOG_LEVEL=DEBUG\n\n# Frontend\nexport VITE_DEBUG=true\n```\n\n#### Access Container Shell\n```bash\n# Backend\ndocker-compose exec backend bash\n\n# Frontend\ndocker-compose exec frontend sh\n\n# PostgreSQL\ndocker-compose exec postgres bash\n```\n\n### Performance Issues\n\n#### Slow Queries\n```sql\n-- PostgreSQL: Enable query logging\nALTER SYSTEM SET log_min_duration_statement = 1000;\nSELECT pg_reload_conf();\n\n-- View slow queries\nSELECT * FROM pg_stat_statements \nWHERE mean_exec_time > 1000 \nORDER BY mean_exec_time DESC;\n```\n\n#### High Memory Usage\n```bash\n# Check container memory\ndocker stats\n\n# Limit container memory\ndocker-compose up -d --scale backend=1 --memory="2g"\n```\n\n### Getting Help\n\n- **Documentation**: Check README.md and API docs at /docs\n- **Logs**: Always check logs first: `docker-compose logs -f`\n- **GitHub Issues**: Report bugs and request features\n- **Community**: Join our Slack/Discord channel\n- **Support**: Email support@itechsmart.dev\n\n---\n\n## Appendix\n\n### Useful Commands\n\n```bash\n# View all containers\ndocker-compose ps\n\n# View resource Integration**: SAML, OAuth2, LDAP support\n- **API Keys**: Programmatic access with API key management\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ›  Technology Stack\n\n### Backend\n- **Framework**: FastAPI 0.109.0 (Python 3.11+)\n- **Database**: PostgreSQL 15 (Primary), ClickHouse (Analytics)\n- **Cache**: Redis 7\n- **Message Queue**: RabbitMQ 3\n- **Object Storage**: MinIO\n- **ORM**: SQLAlchemy 2.0\n- **Authentication**: JWT with OAuth2\n- **API Documentation**: OpenAPI/Swagger\n\n### Frontend\n- **Framework**: React 18 with TypeScript\n- **Build Tool**: Vite 5\n- **UI Library**: Tailwind CSS 3\n- **Charts**: Recharts 2.10\n- **Routing**: React Router 6\n- **State Management**: React Context API\n- **HTTP Client**: Axios\n\n### Infrastructure\n- **Containerization**: Docker 24+, Docker Compose 2+\n- **Orchestration**: Kubernetes (optional)\n- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions, GitLab CI\n- **Monitoring**: Prometheus, Grafana\n- **Logging**: ELK Stack (Elasticsearch, Logstash, Kibana)\n\n### Development Tools\n- **Code Quality**: Black, Flake8, MyPy, ESLint, Prettier\n- **Testing**: Pytest, Jest, React Testing Library\n- **Documentation**: Sphinx, Storybook\n- **Version Control**: Git, GitHub/GitLab\n\n---\n\n## ðŸš€ Quick Start\n\n### Prerequisites\n- Docker 24.0+ and Docker Compose 2.0+\n- 8GB+ RAM (16GB recommended)\n- 20GB+ free disk space\n\n### Installation\n\n1. **Clone the repository**\n```bash\ngit clone <repository-url>\ncd itechsmart-pulse\n```\n\n2. **Configure environment**\n```bash\ncp .env.example .env\n# Edit .env with your configuration\n```\n\n3. **Start all services**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n4. **Access the application**\n- Frontend: http://localhost:5173\n- Backend API: http://localhost:8000\n- API Docs: http://localhost:8000/docs\n\n5. **Login with default credentials**\n```\nEmail: admin@itechsmart.dev\nPassword: password\n```\n\n### First Steps\n\n1. **Connect a Data Source**\n   - Navigate to Data Sources\n   - Click "Add Data Source"\n   - Select your database type\n   - Enter connection details\n   - Test and save\n\n2. **Create a Dataset**\n   - Go to Datasets\n   - Click "New Dataset"\n   - Select your data source\n   - Write or build your query\n   - Save the dataset\n\n3. **Build a Dashboard**\n   - Navigate to Dashboards\n   - Click "Create Dashboard"\n   - Add visualizations\n   - Arrange and configure\n   - Save and share\n\n4. **Generate a Report**\n   - Go to Reports\n   - Click "New Report"\n   - Select dataset and format\n   - Configure schedule (optional)\n   - Generate or schedule\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ— Database Schema\n\n#### PostgreSQL (Primary Database)\n- **users**: User accounts and authentication\n- **data_sources**: Connected data sources\n- **datasets**: Defined datasets and queries\n- **reports**: Report definitions and schedules\n- **dashboards**: Dashboard configurations\n- **visualizations**: Chart and visualization configs\n- **queries**: Saved SQL queries\n- **alerts**: Alert definitions and rules\n- **scheduled_jobs**: Background job schedules\n- **audit_logs**: Complete audit trail\n- **api_keys**: API key management\n\n#### ClickHouse (Analytics Database)\n- **events**: User interaction events\n- **query_metrics**: Query performance metrics\n- **dashboard_views**: Dashboard usage analytics\n- **report_executions**: Report generation logs\n- **data_source_metrics**: Data source performance\n- **alert_triggers**: Alert trigger history\n- **user_activity**: User activity tracking\n- **system_performance**: System metrics\n\n### API Architecture\n\n```\n/api/v1/\nâ”œâ”€â”€ /auth\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST /token              # Login\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST /register           # Register\nâ”‚   â””â”€â”€ GET  /me                 # Current user\nâ”œâ”€â”€ /data-sources\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /                 # List sources\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST   /                 # Create source\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /{id}             # Get /datasets\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /                 # List datasets\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST   /                 # Create dataset\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /{id}             # Get dataset\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /                 # List dashboards\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST   /                 # Create dashboard\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /{id}             # Get dashboard\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ PUT    /{id}             # Update dashboard\nâ”‚   â””â”€â”€ DELETE /{id}             # Delete dashboard\nâ”œâ”€â”€ /reports\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /                 # List reports\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ POST   /                 # Create report\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ GET    /{id}             # Get report\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ PUT    /{id}             # Update report\nâ”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ DELETE /{id}             # Delete report\nâ”‚ metrics\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“š API Documentation\n\n### Interactive Documentation\n- **Swagger UI**: http://localhost:8000/docs\n- **ReDoc**: http://localhost:8000/redoc\n\n### Authentication\n\nAll API endpoints (except `/token` and `/health`) require authentication using JWT Bearer tokens.\n\n#### Get Access Token\n```bash\ncurl -X POST "http://localhost:8000/token" \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded" \\\n  -d "username=admin&password=password"\n```\n\nResponse:\n```json\n{\n  "access_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",\n  "token_type": "bearer",\n  "expires_in": 1800,\n  "user": {\n    "username": "admin",\n    "email": "admin@itechsmart.dev",\n    "role": "admin"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Use Token in Requests\n```bash\ncurl -X GET "http://localhost:8000/data-sources" \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN"\n```\n\n### Example API Calls\n\n#### Create Data Source\n```bash\ncurl -X POST "http://localhost:8000/data-sources" \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN" \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "name": "My Database",\n    "type": "postgresql",\n    "connection_string": "postgresql://user:pass@host:5432/db"\n  }\'\n```\n\n#### Execute Query\n```bash\ncurl -X POST "http://localhost:8000/queries/execute" \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN" \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "sql_query": "SELECT * FROM users LIMIT 10",\n    "data_source_id": "ds_001"\n  }\'\n```\n\n#### Create Dashboard\n```bash\ncurl -X POST "http://localhost:8000/dashboards" \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN" \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "name": "Sales Dashboard",\n    "description": "Monthly sales metrics"\n  }\'\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ’» Development\n\n### Backend Development\n\n#### Setup Local Environment\n```bash\ncd backend\n\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m venv venv\nsource -m "description"\n\n# Apply migrations\ndocker-compose exec backend alembic upgrade head\n\n# Rollback migration\ndocker-compose exec backend alembic downgrade -1\n\n# View migration history\ndocker-compose exec backend alembic history\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸš¢ Deployment\n\n### Docker Compose (Recommended for Development)\n\n```bash\n# Start all services\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n#  """Get request analytics"""\n    cutoff_time = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=hours)\n    \n    recent_logs = [\n        log for log in request_logs\n        if datetime.fromisoformat(log["timestamp"]) > cutoff_time\n    ]\n    \n    # Group by hour\n    hourly_stats = {}\n    for log in recent_logs:\n        hour = log["timestamp"][:13]  # YYYY-MM-DDTHH\n def get_request_logs(\n    skip: int = 0,\n    limit: int = 100,\n    method: Optional[str] = None,\n    status_code: Optional[int] = None,\n    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)\n):\n    """Get request logs"""\n    logs = request_logs.copy()\n    \n    # Filter by method\n    if method:\n        logs = [log for log in logs if log["method"] == method.upper()]\n    \n    # Filter by status code\n    if status_code:\n        logs = [log for log in logs if log["status_code"] == status_code]\n    \n    # Sort by timestamp (newest first)\n    logs.sort(key=lambda x: x["timestamp"], reverse=True)\n    \n    return {\n        "data": logs[skip:skip+limit],\n        "total": len(logs),\n        "skip": skip,\n        "limit": limit\n    }\n\n# finally:\n        db.close()\n\n@contextmanager\ndef get_db_context():\n    """\n    Database session context manager\n    Usage: with get_db_context() as db:\n    """\n    db = SessionLocal()\n    try:\n        yield db\n        db.commit()\n    except Exception:\n        db.rollback()\n        raise\n    finally:\n        db.close()\n\n#  """Redis cache utilities"""\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def get(key: str) -> str:\n        """Get value from cache"""\n        try:\n            return redis_client.get(key)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Redis get error: {e}")\n            return None\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def set(key: str, value: str, expire: int = 3600) -> bool:\n        """Set value in cache with expiration"""\n        try:\n            return redis_client.setex(key, expire, value)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Redis set error: {e}")\n            return           print(f"Redis delete error: {e}")\n            return False\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def exists(key: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if key exists"""\n        try:\n            return = 1) -> int:\n        """Increment counter"""\n        try:\n            return redis_client.incrby(key, amount)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Redis increment error: {e}")\n            return 0\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def expire(key: str, seconds: int) -> bool:\n        """Set expiration on key"""\n        try:\n            return redis_client.expire(key, seconds)\n UTILITIES\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass RateLimiter:\n    """Rate limiting using Redis"""\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def check_rate_limit(\n        identifier: str,\n        limit: int,\n        window_seconds: int = 60\n    ) -> tuple[bool, int]:\n        """\n        Check if rate limit is exceeded\n        Returns: (is_allowed, remaining_requests)\n        """\n        key = f"rate_limit:{identifier}"\n        \n        try:\n            current = redis_client.get(key)\n            \n            if current is None:\n                # First request in window\n                redis_client.setex(key, window_seconds, 1)\n                return True, limit - 1\n            \n            current = int(current)\n            \n            if current >= limit:\n                # Rate limit exceeded\n                ttl = redis_client.ttl(key)\n                return False, 0\n            \n            # Increment counter\n            new_count = redis_client.incr(key)\n            return True, limit - new_count\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Rate limit check error: {e}")\n            # Allow request on error\n            return True, limit\n\n# ============================================================================\n# DATABASE INITIALIZATION\n# Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)\n\ndef drop_db():\n    """Drop all database tables"""\n    from models import Base\n    Base.metadata.drop_all(bind=engine)\n\n#    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    last_login TIMESTAMP\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);\nCREATE INDEX idx_apis_name ON apis USING gin(name gin_trgm_ops);\n\n-- ============================================================================\n-- API ENDPOINTS\n-- ============================================================================\n\nCREATE TABLE api_endpoints (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    api_id UUID REFERENCES apis(id) api_versions(api_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_api_versions_version ON api_versions(version);\n\n-- ============================================================================\n-- API KEYS\n-- ============================================================================\n\nCREATE TABLE api_keys (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    key_hash VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    scopes JSONB DEFAULT \'[]\',\n    rate_limit INTEGER DEFAULT 1000,\n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT  -d "username=admin&password=password"\n```\n\n#### Use Token in Requests\n```bash\ncurl -X GET "http://localhost:8000/apis" \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN"\n```\n\n### Key connect_user connect > backup.sql\n\n# Restore database\ndocker-compose exec -T postgres psql -U connect_user connect < backup.sql\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸš¢ Deployment\n\n### Docker Compose
